CREATE TABLE `filmler` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `filmadi` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `yonetmen` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `senarist` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `yil` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `oyuncular` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `orjinaladi` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `ozet` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `poster` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `dil` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `turler` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `tagline` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `puan` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `etiketler` text DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=401 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;
